*testing.T) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tcfg = defaultConfig()\n\t\treq = httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://example.com/foo\", nil)\n\t\tw   = httptest.NewRecorder()\n\t)\n\n\tcfg.ServeHTTP(w, req)\n\n\tresp
